            no update of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source
            content</a> and its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-descendant">descendants</a> is performed.
          </p>
          <p>
            The <var>timeline time</var> used in the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event
            dispatch</a> procedure is simply the <var>seek time</var>.
          </p>
          <p>
            After completing the seek, the previous sample time of the
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> is updated to reflect the <var>seek time</var> and the
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a>, if set, is cleared.
          </p>
          <p class="annotation">
            Suppressing events during seeking is necessary to provide performant
            seeking.
            It is also arguably the more intuitive behavior as, for example,
            when rewinding a cartoon one probably does not expect a bucketload
            of events to arrive as a result of traversing backwards over each
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
          </p>
        </div>
        <div class="section" id="event-dispatch-and-time-adjustments">
          <h4><span class="secno">5.7.3 </span>Event dispatch and time adjustments</h4>
          <div class="informative informative-bg">
            <p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p><p>
              Apart from seeking a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>, making adjustments to the
              arrangement or timing of a player's <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> can also
              cause the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a>' <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-local-time">local time</a> to jump.
              Like seeking, in such circumstances it is often not sensible to
              dispatch all the intermediate events but rather to employ
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event dispatch</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The range of circumstances where this behavior is necessary is
              quite broad when we consider the interdependencies in the timing
              of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a>.
              For example,
            </p>
            <ul>
              <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">Timing groups</a> calculate their <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-intrinsic-iteration-duration">intrinsic iteration
              duration</a> based on the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a> of their
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item" title="child timed item">children</a>.</li>
              <li>Children of a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sequence-timing-group">sequence timing group</a> base their
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-start-time" title="timed item start time">start time</a> on the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active
              duration</a> of sibling <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> that appear earlier in
              the group.</li>
            </ul>
            <p>
              As such, even small changes to the timing of a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
              can have knock-on effects that affect all other <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a>
              <a title="associated with a player">associated</a> with the same
              player possibly causing their <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-local-time">local time</a> to jump.
              As a result, <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event dispatch</a> is employed for the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> of a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> and <em>all</em> its
              descendents whenever <em>any</em> change is made to the timing or
              arrangement of any of those <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a>.
            </p>
          </div>
          <p>
            Associated with each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> is a <dfn id="dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted
            flag</dfn> that is initially <code>false</code>.
          </p>
          <p>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a> is set to <code>true</code> whenever
            any of the following actions is performed on any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
            items</a> <a title="associated with a player">associated</a> with
            the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
          </p>
          <ul>
            <li>The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a> changes identity including
                changes to and from <code>null</code>.
                This includes <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> that become newly <a title="associated with a player">associated</a> with the
                <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> or likewise cease to be associated with the
                player.</li>
            <li>
              The following timing parameters are modified:
              <ul>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start delay</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-start">iteration start</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-count">iteration count</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-playback-rate" title="timed item playback rate">playback rate</a></li>
                <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-playback-direction">playback direction</a></li>
              </ul>
              <p class="note">
                Note that the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-fill-mode">fill mode</a> and <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-function">timing function</a>
                associated with a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> are not included in this
                list since they do not effect <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-timing">uneased timing</a>.
              </p>
              <p>
                This behavior extends only to actual changes to the
                values.
                Setting a property to its current value&#x2014;for example, by
                using the <a href="#script-interface">script
                interface</a>&#x2014; does <em>not</em> cause the flag to be set.
              </p>
            </li>
            <li>
              The sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item" title="child timed item">children</a> within
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing group</a> is changed.
            </li>
          </ul>
          <p>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a> is cleared after <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-events-are-queued">events are
            queued</a> for the given <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
          </p>
          <p>
            When <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-events-are-queued" title="events are queued">queuing events</a> for
            a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>, if the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a> of the
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> is set, <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event dispatch</a> is used for all
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> <a title="associated with
            a player">associated</a> with the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
          </p>
        </div>
        <div class="section" id="event-dispatch-and-unattached-timed-items">
          <h4><span class="secno">5.7.4 </span>Event dispatch and unattached timed items</h4>
          <div class="issue">
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a> event may not be necessary.
            </p>
            <p>
              It was introduced since in some situations it is useful to
              distinguish between an animation completing normally
              (<a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a>&#x2014;in which case actions that are scheduled
              to occur at the end of the animation should be performed) and
              being prematurely terminated (<a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a>&#x2014;in which
              case such actions will generally not be performed).
            </p>
            <p>
              Currently the only way to prematurely end a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> is
              to manually disassociate it from any <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> which seems too
              rare to warrant a special event.
              If <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">players</a> could be cancelled or stopped in some way then
              this event may make more sense.
            </p>
            <p>
              Note that the <em>touchcancel</em> event is conceptually similar
              and may be an argument in favor of keeping this event.
            </p>
          </div>
          <p>
            A <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> that is not <a>associated with a player</a> is
            an <dfn id="dfn-unattached-timed-item">unattached timed item</dfn>.
          </p>
          <p>
            Each time an operation is performed that causes a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
            that was <a>associated with a player</a> to become an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-unattached-timed-item">unattached
            timed item</a> it is appended to the end of a <dfn id="dfn-queue-of-unattached-timed-items">queue of
            unattached timed items</dfn> associated with the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
          </p>
          <p>
            Should an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-unattached-timed-item">unattached timed item</a> later become <a>associated
            with a player</a> it is removed from any <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-queue-of-unattached-timed-items">queue of unattached
            timed items</a> it may be present in.
            As a result a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> will only ever appear in at most one
            <a>queue of unattached times</a> and never twice in the same queue.
          </p>
          <p>
            When <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-events-are-queued">events are queued</a> as a result of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sampling">sampling</a>,
            the following steps are performed for all <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in the
            <a>queue of unattached items</a> for each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> that is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sampling" title="sampling">sampled</a>.
          </p>
          <ol>
            <li>If the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> is
                <em>active</em>,
                <ol>
                  <li>Queue a new <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a> event with all parameters
                      set to <code>null</code>.</li>
                  <li>Set the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a> to
                      <em>inactive</em>.</li>
                </ol>
            </li>
            <li>
              Remove the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> from the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-queue-of-unattached-timed-items">queue of unattached timed
              items</a>.
            </li>
          </ol>
          <p class="note">
            Note that <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a> events are not dispatched when <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeking" title="seeking">seeking</a> a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
            As a result it is possible, using the <a href="#script-interface">script interface</a> to make a batch of
            changes to the arrangement of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> including
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeking">seeking</a> and provided all <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> are <a>associated
            with a player</a> when the script block completes no
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a> events will be dispatched.
          </p>
        </div>
        <div class="section" id="event-dispatch-and-extended-delays">
          <h4><span class="secno">5.7.5 </span>Event dispatch and extended delays</h4>
          <div class="informative informative-bg">
            <p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p><p>
              In some circumstances, when <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-events-are-queued">events are queued</a> during
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sample">sample</a>, the number of events generated may be excessive.
              This can happen, for example, if the user agent dramatically
              reduces the sample rate for a background application to conserve
              battery, or if the device is activated after being in a sleep
              state for an extended period of time.
            </p>
            <p>
              In such situations, requiring the user agent to dispatch all
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing events</a> scheduled in the interim period would result
              in a significant drop in performance and in extreme circumstances
              may render the user agent temporarily unusable whilst it catches
              up on event processing.
            </p>
            <p>
              In order to ensure a good user experience even in such
              circumstances a user agent may switch to <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event
              dispatch</a> to alleviate the burden of dispatching excessive
              events.
            </p>
          </div>
          <p>
            If, whilst <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sampling">sampling</a> a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a>, more than 30 <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-events-are-queued">events
            are queued</a>, the user agent <em title="may" class="rfc2119">may</em> employ <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-event-dispatch">seeked event
            dispatch</a> for all <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-associated-with-a-timeline" title="associated with a timeline">associated</a> with the
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a>.
          </p>
          <p class="issue">
            30 is somewhat arbitrary.
            Need feedback both from implementations (on the most constrained
            device, when does this start being burdensome?) and authoring (what
            is the minimum guarantee necessary to cover most regular content?)
          </p>
          <div class="annotation">
            The SVG bindings may add additional requirements here so that when
            a protracted delay may make resolving syncbase dependencies in the
            interim period difficult to achieve without adversely impacting
            performance, a seek is performed.
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="section" id="script-interface">
      <!--OddPage--><h2><span class="secno">6. </span>Script interface</h2>
      <div class="informative informative-bg">
        <p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p><p>
          In addition to the abstract model described above, Web Animations also
          defines a programming interface to the model.
          This interface can be used to inspect and extend animations produced
          by declarative means or for directly producing animations when
          a procedural approach is more suitable.
        </p>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timeline-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.1 </span>The <code>Timeline</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">Timelines</a>, including the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-document-timeline">document
          timeline</a> are represented in the Web Animations API by the
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline" title="Timeline interface"><code>Timeline</code></a> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-Timeline">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">Timeline</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a>?</span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timeline-currentTime">currentTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a></span>           <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-Timeline-play-Player-TimedItem-source">play</a></span> (<span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span> <span class="idlParamName">source</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">null</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType">sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a>&gt;</span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-Timeline-getCurrentPlayers-sequence-Player">getCurrentPlayers</a></span> ();</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>double</a>?</span>          <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-Timeline-toTimelineTime-double-double-otherTime-Timeline-other">toTimelineTime</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>double</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">otherTime</span></span>, <span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline"><code>Timeline</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">other</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>double</a>?</span>          <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-Timeline-toTimelineTime-double-Event-event">toTimelineTime</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>Event</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">event</span></span>);</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes"><h4><span class="secno">6.1.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-Timeline-currentTime"><code>currentTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> for this timeline or
              <code>null</code> if this timeline is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-not-started">not started</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              For a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-document-timeline">document timeline</a> this will never be negative and
              represents the number of seconds since the document with which
              this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> is associated was ready to fire its load
              event.
            </p>
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods"><h4><span class="secno">6.1.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-Timeline-play-Player-TimedItem-source"><code>play</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> object
              associated with this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> that is scheduled to start
              at <code>currentTime</code>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The <code>timeline</code> attribute of the newly-created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> object will be set to this
              object.
            </p>
            <p>
              Similarly, the <code>startTime</code> attribute will be set to the
              value of this object's <code>currentTime</code> attribute at the
              moment the method was called, or, if <code>currentTime</code> is
              <code>null</code>, zero.
            </p>
            <p>
              The setting of the <code>source</code> attribute is described
              below under the description of the <em>source</em> parameter.
            </p>
            <p>
              The <code>currentTime</code> attribute of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player
              interface"><code>Player</code></a> object is a calculated value described in <a href="#the-current-time-of-a-player" class="sectionRef">section 3.5.1 The current time of a player</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The <code>playbackRate</code> and <code>paused</code> attributes
              take on their default values as described in the definitions of
              the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player-playback-rate" title="player playback rate">playback rate</a> and
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-paused-state">paused state</a> properties of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> objects.
            </p>
            
            <div class="issue">
              <p>
                We will likely change this interface to the following format:
              </p>
              <pre class="example webidl">Promise play(optional TimedItem? source = null);
Player  playNow(optional TimedItem? source = null);</pre>
              <p>
                Under this arrangement <code>play</code> would begin at the next
                possible moment whilst attempting to ensure that the animation
                begins from the first frame.
                This allows implementations to make adjustments for vsync or
                overhead in triggering the animation in another process.
              </p>
              <p>
                The <code>play</code> callback passes the created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> as the argument to the
                Promise's fulfill callback.
              </p>
              <p>
                <code>playNow</code> matches the existing definition of the
                function and causes the start time of the player to be set to
                this timeline's <code>currentTime</code> even though this may
                cause the first part of the animation to be dropped.
              </p>
            </div>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">source</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>null</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc">
                <p>
                  The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> to assign to the newly-created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> object.
                </p>
                <p>
                  The <a href="#widl-Player-source"><code>source</code></a>
                  attribute of the created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player
                  interface"><code>Player</code></a> is set by following the procedure
                  defined for updating that attribute.
                  As a result, if <em>source</em> is already associated with
                  a <code>player</code>, it will be disassociated first before
                  being associated with the new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player
                  interface"><code>Player</code></a> object.
                </p>
              </td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a></code></div></dd><dt id="widl-Timeline-getCurrentPlayers-sequence-Player"><code>getCurrentPlayers</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the set of <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> objects
              associated with this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> that have associated
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> which is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current">current</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The returned list is sorted in increasing order of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player-start-time" title="player start time">start time</a> of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player
              interface"><code>Player</code></a> objects.
              If any two <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> objects have the
              same <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player-start-time" title="player start time">start time</a> they are sorted
              in the order in which the objects were created.
            </p>
            <div class="issue">
              <p>
                Does this ordering make sense?
              </p>
              <p>
                Ordering by creation order only is simpler and useful for the
                case of fetching the most recently created player (e.g. when you
                call a utility function that plays an animation but
                inconsiderately does not return the player) but that doesn't
                work for <code>Element.getCurrentPlayers</code> (unless we make
                creation order global?) and the two methods should probably use
                consistent ordering.
              </p>
            </div>
          <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code>sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a>&gt;</code></div></dd><dt id="widl-Timeline-toTimelineTime-double-double-otherTime-Timeline-other"><code>toTimelineTime</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a>, <em>otherTime</em>, from another
              <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline" title="Timeline interface"><code>Timeline</code></a> also tied to the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-global-clock">global clock</a>, <em>other</em>, converted to a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time
              value</a> relative to this timeline's <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-zero-time">zero time</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Returns <code>null</code> if:
            </p>
            <ul>
              <li>this timeline is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-not-started">not started</a>, or</li>
              <li><em>other</em> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-not-started">not started</a>.</li>
            </ul>
            <p>
              Note that unlike <code>currentTime</code>, this method may return
              a negative <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> if <em>otherTime</em> occurred prior
              to this timeline's <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-zero-time">zero time</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Furthermore, negative values for <em>otherTime</em> are also
              allowed.
            </p>
            <p>
              If this timeline records the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-global-clock">global
              clock</a> at its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-zero-time">zero time</a> as <var>global clock
              offset</var>, and so does <em>other</em> as <var>other global
              clock offset</var>, then the result of this method is simply:
            </p>
            <blockquote>
              <code><var>other global clock offset</var> + <var>otherTime</var>
              - <var>global clock offset</var></code>
            </blockquote>
            <p>
              Exceptions:
            </p>
            <dl class="exceptions">
              <dt>DOMException of type <code>InvalidNodeTypeError</code></dt>
              <dd>
                Raised if <em>other</em> is a timeline that is not tied to the
                <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-global-clock">global clock</a>.
                <p class="annotation">
                  The reason for choosing <code>InvalidNodeTypeError</code> here
                  is that DOM4 describes it as meaning, "The supplied node is
                  incorrect or has an incorrect ancestor for this operation."
                  In this case the error is because <em>other</em> does not have
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-global-clock">global clock</a> as an ancestor so it seems
                  appropriate.
                </p>
              </dd>
            </dl>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">otherTime</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>double</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">other</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline"><code>Timeline</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>double</a></code>, nullable</div></dd><dt id="widl-Timeline-toTimelineTime-double-Event-event"><code>toTimelineTime</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the number of seconds between when <em>event</em> was
              fired and this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a>'s <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-zero-time">zero time</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Since the <code>timeStamp</code> attribute of the
              <code>Event</code> interface specified in [<cite><a href="#bib-DOM-LEVEL-3-EVENTS" rel="biblioentry" class="bibref">DOM-LEVEL-3-EVENTS</a></cite>]
              is not guaranteed to be monotonically increasing, implementations
              <em title="should" class="rfc2119">should</em> record alongside each event the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> of the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-global-clock">global clock</a> when the event is dispatched so that it can be
              converted to an accurate <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> here.
            </p>
            <p>
              Unlike <code>currentTime</code>, this method may return a negative
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> if the event was fired prior to this
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a>'s <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-zero-time">zero time</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Returns <code>null</code> if this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-not-started">not
              started</a>.
            </p>
            <p class="issue">
              This might be deferred to a later version.
            </p>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">event</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>Event</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>double</a></code>, nullable</div></dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-player-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.2 </span>The <code>Player</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">Players</a> are represented in the Web Animations
          API by the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player" title="Player interface"><code>Player</code></a> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-Player">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">Player</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-source">source</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline"><code>Timeline</code></a></span>   <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-timeline">timeline</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>     <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-startTime">startTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>     <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-currentTime">currentTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>     <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-playbackRate">playbackRate</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>boolean</a></span>    <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Player-paused">paused</a></span>;</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-1"><h4><span class="secno">6.2.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-Player-source"><code>source</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span>, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> associated with this player.
            </p>
            <p>
              A <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> can only be associated with at most one <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a>, and likewise, a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> can only be
              associated&#x2014;either directly or via an
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-ancestor">ancestor</a>&#x2014;with at most one <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
              In order to maintain these invariants, on setting this value, the
              following procedure is performed:
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>Let <var>old value</var> be the current value of the
                  <code>source</code> attribute.</li>
              <li>Let <var>new value</var> be the value to set.</li>
              <li>If <var>new value</var> is the same object as <var>old
                  value</var>, return.</li>
              <li>If <var>old value</var> is not <code>null</code>,
                  disassociate <var>old value</var> from this player.</li>
              <li>If <var>new value</var> is not <code>null</code>,
                  perform the steps associated with the first matching condition
                  of the following:
                <dl class="switch">
                  <dt>If <var>new value</var> has no parent group and is
                      associated with a player,</dt>
                  <dd>disassociate <var>new value</var> from its player.</dd>
                  <dt>If <var>new value</var> has a parent group,</dt>
                  <dd>remove <var>new value</var> from its parent group by
                      calling <code><var>new value</var>.remove()</code>.</dd>
                  <dt>Otherwise,</dt>
                  <dd>do nothing.</dd>
                </dl>
              </li>
              <li>Associate <var>new value</var> with this player.
              </li><li>Set the <code>source</code> attribute to <var>new
                  value</var>.</li>
            </ol>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Player-timeline"><code>timeline</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timeline"><code>Timeline</code></a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> associated with this player.
          </dd><dt id="widl-Player-startTime"><code>startTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player-start-time" title="player start time">start time</a> of this player.
          </dd><dt id="widl-Player-currentTime"><code>currentTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-effective-current-time">effective current time</a> of this player.
            Setting this attribute follows the procedure defined in <a href="#performing-a-seek" class="sectionRef">section 3.5.2.6 Performing a seek</a>.
          </dd><dt id="widl-Player-playbackRate"><code>playbackRate</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player-playback-rate" title="player playback rate">playback rate</a> of this
            player.
            Setting this attribute follows the procedure defined in <a href="#updating-the-playback-rate" class="sectionRef">section 3.5.3.1 Updating the playback rate</a>.
          </dd><dt id="widl-Player-paused"><code>paused</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>boolean</a></span></dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-paused-state">paused state</a> of this player.
            Setting this attribute follows the procedure defined in <a href="#updating-the-paused-state" class="sectionRef">section 3.5.2.5 Updating the paused state</a>.
          </dd></dl></div>
        <div class="feedbackWanted">
          <p>
            A reverse method would be very useful here for effects like
            transitions.
          </p>
          <p>
            The behavior would be:
          </p>
          <ol>
            <li>If <code>currentTime</code> is beyond the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-end-time">end
                time</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> seek back to the end of
                the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-interval">active interval</a>.
            </li><li>Set <code>playbackRate</code> to
                <code>-playbackRate</code>.</li>
          </ol>
          <p>
            This reflects how transitions work as well as common usage.
          </p>
          <p>
            Some objections:
          </p>
          <ul>
            <li>Calling <code>reverse</code> twice should be a noop.</li>
            <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">Players</a> should be independent of their
                <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a>.</li>
          </ul>
          <p>
            Some suggestions:
          </p>
          <ul>
            <li>Call it <code>reverseSource</code> to make the link to the the
                <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> obvious and remove any expectation that
                calling it twice is a noop.</li>
            <li>Make <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">players</a> actually stop when they reach
                the end of their <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a> much like a video/DVD/CD
                player.
                This would eliminate the need for the reverse seek and would
                make calling twice a noop.</li>
          </ul>
          <p>
            Your feedback is most welcome at <a href="mailto:public-fx@w3.org">public-fx@w3.org</a>, subject
            <em>[web-anim] &#x2026;</em>.
          </p>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timeditem-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.3 </span>The <code>TimedItem</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">Timed items</a> are represented in the Web
          Animations API by the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-TimedItem">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">TimedItem</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a>EventTarget</a></span> {
<span class="idlSectionComment">    // Playback state</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a>?</span>             <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-localTime">localTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unsigned long</a>?</span>      <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-currentIteration">currentIteration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlSectionComment">
    // Specified timing</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a></span>              <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-specified">specified</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlSectionComment">
    // Calculated timing</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>              <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-startTime">startTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-iterationDuration">iterationDuration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-activeDuration">activeDuration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-endTime">endTime</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlSectionComment">
    // Timing hierarchy</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a>?</span>        <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-parent">parent</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span>          <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-previousSibling">previousSibling</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span>          <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-nextSibling">nextSibling</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-before-void-TimedItem...-items">before</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>TimedItem...</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">items</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-after-void-TimedItem...-items">after</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>TimedItem...</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">items</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-replace-void-TimedItem...-items">replace</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>TimedItem...</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">items</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-remove-void">remove</a></span> ();</span>
<span class="idlSectionComment">
    // Associated player</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a>?</span>             <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-player">player</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlSectionComment">
    // Event callbacks</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span>        <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-onstart">onstart</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span>        <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-oniteration">oniteration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span>        <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-onend">onend</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span>        <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItem-oncancel">oncancel</a></span>;</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-2"><h4><span class="secno">6.3.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-TimedItem-localTime"><code>localTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-local-time">local time</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              <code>localTime</code> will be <code>null</code> if this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a> is not directly or indirectly associated with
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> or if it has a parent <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing group</a> that is
              not <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-effect">in effect</a>.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-currentIteration"><code>currentIteration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unsigned long</a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-iteration">current iteration</a> index beginning with zero for the first
            iteration.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-specified"><code>specified</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the input timing properties for this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <div class="feedbackWanted">
              <p>
                Representing these parameters has been a particularly
                contentious topic.
              </p>
              <p>
                The current arrangement:
              </p>
              <ul>
                <li>requires defining both a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface and
                    a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> dictionary type which increases the API
                    surface area somewhat
                </li><li>means that setting the value occurs at a different place
                    (<code>anim.specified.iterationDuration</code>) to reading
                    the value (typically, <code>anim.iterationDuration</code>)
                </li><li>opens up questions about whether <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> objects
                    should be share-able or not
                </li><li>uses a union of a string and a double to represent
                    a duration which opens up questions about whether strings
                    such as <code>"3s"</code> should be allowed (and allowing
                    them makes walking the tree more complex).
              </li></ul>
              <p>
                However, it separates "specified" timing from "computed" timing
                which some consider advantageous.
              </p>
              <p>
                The only situation where calculated values and input values
                differ is for <code>iterationDuration</code> and
                <code>activeDuration</code>.
              </p>
              <p>
                One alternative that has been proposed is to introduce
                a <code>Duration</code> interface as follows:
              </p>
              <pre class="example webidl">interface TimedItem : EventTarget {
   // Timing
   attribute double   startDelay;
   attribute FillMode fillMode;
   attribute Duration iterationDuration;
   attribute Duration activeDuration;
   attribute double   playbackRate;
   // ...
   
   // Scheduled time
   readonly attribute double              startTime;
   readonly attribute unrestricted double endTime;
};

interface Duration {
  double    sec;
  DOMString string;
}</pre>
              <p>
                Usage is as follows:
              </p>
              <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_keyword">var</span> specifiedDur  <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>string<span class="sh_symbol">;</span> <span class="sh_comment">// "auto"</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> calculatedDur <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>sec<span class="sh_symbol">;</span> <span class="sh_comment">// 5</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Update duration to 3s</span>
anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>sec <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>
<span class="sh_comment">// anim.iterationDuration.string -&gt; "3s"</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Update duration to 3s (alt.)</span>
anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>string <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_string">"3s"</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>
<span class="sh_comment">// anim.iterationDuration.sec -&gt; 3</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Reset to auto</span>
anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>string <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_string">"auto"</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>  
<span class="sh_comment">// anim.iterationDuration.sec -&gt; 5</span></pre>
              <p>
                Your feedback is most welcome at <a href="mailto:public-fx@w3.org">public-fx@w3.org</a>, subject
                <em>[web-anim] &#x2026;</em>.
              </p>
            </div>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-startTime"><code>startTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a>start time</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> in seconds.
              This is the time at which the parent <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing group</a>, if any,
              has scheduled this child to run within its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-transformed-time" title="transformed
              time">transformed time space</a>, that is, the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>'s
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inherited-time" title="inherited time">inherited time space</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The start of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-interval">active interval</a> is based on the sum of
              the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-start-time" title="timed item start time">start time</a> and
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start delay</a>.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-iterationDuration"><code>iterationDuration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Unlike the <code>iterationDuration</code> attribute of
              the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> dictionary,
              this attribute returns the calculated value of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration
              duration</a>.
              If <code>specified.iterationDuration</code> is the
              string <code>auto</code> or any unsupported value, this attribute
              will return the current calculated value of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-intrinsic-iteration-duration">intrinsic
              iteration duration</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              This value may be changed by setting the
              <code>iterationDuration</code> attribute of the
              <code>specified</code> member of this interface.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-activeDuration"><code>activeDuration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              As with <code>iterationDuration</code>, this attribute returns the
              calculated value of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a>.
              If <code>specified.activeDuration</code> is the
              string <code>auto</code> or any unsupported value,
              this is the result of evaluating the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a> using
              the procedure defined in <a href="#calculating-the-active-duration" class="sectionRef">section 3.10.2 Calculating the active duration</a>.
              Otherwise, it is the value specified for
              <code>specified.activeDuration</code>.
            </p>
            <p>
              This value may be changed by setting the
              <code>activeDuration</code> attribute of the
              <code>specified</code> member of this interface.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-endTime"><code>endTime</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The upper bound of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-interval">active interval</a> expressed in
              seconds in <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inherited-time" title="inherited time">inherited time space</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              <code>endTime</code> is calculated as
              <code><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-start-time" title="timed item start time">start time</a> + <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start
                    delay</a> + activeDuration</code>
            </p>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that while the <code>endTime</code> is read-only, it can be
                set indirectly as follows:
              </p>
              <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_comment">// Set endTime to 't'</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> t <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_number">6</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>
timing<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>specified<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>activeDuration <span class="sh_symbol">=</span>
  t <span class="sh_symbol">-</span> anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>startTime <span class="sh_symbol">-</span> anim<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>specified<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>startDelay<span class="sh_symbol">;</span></pre>
            </div>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-parent"><code>parent</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> or
              <code>null</code> if this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> does not have
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>.
            </p>
            <div class="issue">
              Should this be <code>parentGroup</code>?
            </div>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-previousSibling"><code>previousSibling</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-sibling">previous sibling</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-nextSibling"><code>nextSibling</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-next-sibling">next sibling</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-player"><code>player</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Player"><code>Player</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> associated with this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a>&#x2014;either <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-directly-associated-with-a-player" title="directly associated with a player">directly</a> or
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-indirectly-associated-with-a-player" title="indirectly associated with a player">indirectly</a>.
              This object can be used to perform play control such as pausing or
              rewinding on this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> <em>and all other timed items
              in the same hierarchy</em>.
            </p>
            <p>
              This method will return <code>null</code> if this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a> is not associated with a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-onstart"><code>onstart</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span></dt><dd>
            The event handler for the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingstart">timingstart</a> event.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-oniteration"><code>oniteration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span></dt><dd>
            The event handler for the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingiteration">timingiteration</a> event.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-onend"><code>onend</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span></dt><dd>
            The event handler for the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a> event.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-oncancel"><code>oncancel</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>EventHandler</a></span></dt><dd>
            The event handler for the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingcancel">timingcancel</a> event.
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-1"><h4><span class="secno">6.3.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-TimedItem-before-void-TimedItem...-items"><code>before</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Inserts <var>items</var> before this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>If there is no <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>, terminate these
                  steps.
              </li><li>If any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in <var>items</var> is an
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                  throw a <code>HierarchyRequestError</code> exception and
                  terminate these steps. 
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">Insert</a> <var>items</var> before
                  this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </li></ol>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that this definition precludes the following usage since
                <code>item</code> is an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of itself:
              </p>
              <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode">item<span class="sh_symbol">.</span><span class="sh_function">before</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>item<span class="sh_symbol">);</span> <span class="sh_comment">// throws HierarchyRequestError</span></pre>
            </div>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">items</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>TimedItem...</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-after-void-TimedItem...-items"><code>after</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Inserts <var>items</var> after this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>.
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>If there is no <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>, terminate these
                  steps.
              </li><li>If any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in <var>items</var> is an
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                  throw a <code>HierarchyRequestError</code> exception and
                  terminate these steps. 
              </li><li>Let <var>reference child</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-next-sibling-not-included" title="next sibling not included">next sibling of
                  this timed item not in <var>items</var></a>.
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">Insert</a> <var>items</var> before
                  <var>reference child</var>.
            </li></ol>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">items</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>TimedItem...</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-replace-void-TimedItem...-items"><code>replace</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Replaces this <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> with the passed in
              <var>items</var>.
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>If there is no <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>, terminate these
                  steps.
              </li><li>If any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in <var>items</var> is an
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>
                  throw a <code>HierarchyRequestError</code> exception and
                  terminate these steps. 
              </li><li>Let <var>reference child</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-next-sibling-not-included" title="next sibling not included">next sibling of
                  this timed item not in <var>items</var></a>.
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-remove-a-timed-item" title="remove a timed item">Remove</a> this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
                  item</a> from its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>.
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">Insert</a> <var>items</var> before
                  <var>reference child</var>.
            </li></ol>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">items</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>TimedItem...</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd><dt id="widl-TimedItem-remove-void"><code>remove</code></dt><dd>
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-remove-a-timed-item" title="remove a timed item">Removes</a> this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
            item</a> from its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>.
          <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
        <p class="note">
          Note that the <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/html5/webappapis.html#eventhandler">EventHandler</a>
          callback interface type is defined in [<cite><a href="#bib-HTML5" rel="biblioentry" class="bibref">HTML5</a></cite>].
        </p>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timing-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.4 </span>The <code>Timing</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          Timing parameters for a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> are collected together under
          the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> type.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-Timing">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">Timing</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-startDelay">startDelay</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a></span>                           <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-fillMode">fillMode</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-iterationStart">iterationStart</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>                <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-iterationCount">iterationCount</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-iterationDuration">iterationDuration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-activeDuration">activeDuration</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-playbackRate">playbackRate</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PlaybackDirection"><code>PlaybackDirection</code></a></span>                  <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-direction">direction</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>DOMString</a></span>                          <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Timing-timingFunction">timingFunction</a></span>;</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-3"><h4><span class="secno">6.4.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-Timing-startDelay"><code>startDelay</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start delay</a> which represents the number of seconds from
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>'s <a title="start time">start time</a> to the
              start of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-interval">active interval</a>.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-fillMode"><code>fillMode</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-fill-mode">fill mode</a> as specified by one of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a>
              enumeration values.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-iterationStart"><code>iterationStart</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a><a>'s </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-start">iteration start</a> property.
            </p>
            <p>
              A finite real number greater than or equal to zero representing
              the number of iterations into the timed item at which to begin.
              For example, a value of 0.5 would cause the timed item to begin
              half-way through the first iteration.
            </p>
            <p>
              Values less than zero are clamped to zero for the purpose of
              timing model calculations.
            </p>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that the <code>iterationCount</code> is effectively
                <em>added</em> to the <code>iterationStart</code> such that
                a timed item with an <code>iterationStart</code> of
                &#x2018;0.5&#x2019; and <code>iterationCount</code> of
                &#x2018;2&#x2019; would still repeat twice however it would begin
                and end half-way through the timed item's <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-interval">iteration
                interval</a>.
              </p>
              <p>
                Setting the <code>iterationStart</code> to a value greater than
                or equal to one is typically only useful in combination with an
                animation effect that has an <code>accumulate</code> property of
                &#x2018;accumulate&#x2019;.
              </p>
            </div>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-iterationCount"><code>iterationCount</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a><a>'s </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-count">iteration count</a> property.
            </p>
            <p>
              A real number greater than or equal to zero (including positive
              infinity) representing the number of times to repeat the
              timed item.
            </p>
            <p>
              Values less than zero are treated as the value 1.0 for the purpose
              of timing model calculations.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-iterationDuration"><code>iterationDuration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> which is a real number greater than
              or equal to zero (including positive infinity) representing the
              time taken to complete a single iteration of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The string value <code>auto</code> is used to indicate that the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> reflects the timed item's <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-intrinsic-iteration-duration">intrinsic
              iteration duration</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Real numbers less than zero and strings other than the value
              lowercase value <code>auto</code> are treated the same as
              <code>auto</code> for the purpose of timing model calculations.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-activeDuration"><code>activeDuration</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>, that is, the
              length of its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-interval">active interval</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              The string value <code>auto</code> is used to indicate that the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active duration</a> is calculated using the procedure defined
              in <a href="#calculating-the-active-duration" class="sectionRef">section 3.10.2 Calculating the active duration</a>.
              Otherwise, if a real number greater than or equal to zero
              (including positive infinity) is specified, that procedure is
              ignored and the value provided here is used for all timing model
              calculations that refer to the active duration.
            </p>
            <p>
              Real numbers less than zero and strings other than the value
              lowercase value <code>auto</code> are treated the same as
              <code>auto</code> for the purpose of timing model calculations.
            </p>
            <div class="issue">
              <p>Should we allow strings such as <code>"3s"</code> here?
              i.e. a CSS <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-values/#time">&lt;time&gt;</a>.
              It might be useful for readability but introduces complexity when
              handling this member (need to test the type, then possibly parse
              the string).
              It also introduces the issue of whether we should parse a full
              <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/SVG11/animate.html#ClockValueSyntax">clock
              value</a>.
            </p></div>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-playbackRate"><code>playbackRate</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>double</a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a><a>'s </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-playback-rate" title="timed item playback rate">playback rate</a> property.
            </p>
            <p>
              This is a multiplier applied to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-local-time">local time</a> potentially
              causing the item to run at a different rate to its natural speed.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-direction"><code>direction</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PlaybackDirection"><code>PlaybackDirection</code></a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-playback-direction">playback direction</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> as
              specified by one of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PlaybackDirection"><code>PlaybackDirection</code></a> enumeration
              values.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Timing-timingFunction"><code>timingFunction</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>DOMString</a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-function">timing function</a> used to scale the time to
              produce easing effects.
            </p>
            <p>
              The acceptable values and their meanings are those defined for the
              <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-transitions/#transition-timing-function-property">transition-timing-function</a>
              property in CSS Transitions [<cite><a href="#bib-CSS3-TRANSITIONS" rel="biblioentry" class="bibref">CSS3-TRANSITIONS</a></cite>].
            </p>
            <p>
              In addition to the values defined in CSS Transitions, this method
              extends the <code>steps()</code> function notation to allow
              &#x2018;middle&#x2019; as a transition point keyword (e.g.
              <code>steps(3, middle)</code>).
              Similarly, the keyword &#x2018;steps-middle&#x2019; is recognized
              and given the meaning <code>steps(1, middle)</code>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Strings that specify a <code>cubic-bezier()</code> timing function
