              result produce a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-cubic-b-zier-timing-function">cubic B&#xe9;zier timing function</a>.
              Strings that specify a <code>steps()</code> function produce a
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-step-timing-function">step timing function</a>. Strings that specify a<code>paced()</code>
              timing function result produce a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-paced-timing-function">paced timing function</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              Unrecognized string values are treated as if the
              <code>linear</code> keyword was specified for the purpose of
              timing model calculations.
            </p>
          </dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timinginput-dictionary">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.5 </span>The <code>TimingInput</code> dictionary</h3>
        <p>
          The <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> dictionary is used as a convenience for
          specifying the timing properties of a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> in bulk.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlDictionary" id="idl-def-TimingInput">dictionary <span class="idlDictionaryID">TimingInput</span> {
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-startDelay">startDelay</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">0</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a></span>                           <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-fillMode">fillMode</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">"forwards"</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-iterationStart">iterationStart</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">0.0</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>                <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-iterationCount">iterationCount</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">1.0</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span> <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-iterationDuration">iterationDuration</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">"auto"</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span> <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-activeDuration">activeDuration</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">"auto"</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a>double</a></span>                             <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-playbackRate">playbackRate</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">1.0</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PlaybackDirection"><code>PlaybackDirection</code></a></span>                  <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-direction">direction</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">"normal"</span>;</span>
<span class="idlMember">    <span class="idlMemberType"><a>DOMString</a></span>                          <span class="idlMemberName"><a href="#widl-TimingInput-timingFunction">timingFunction</a></span> = <span class="idlMemberValue">"linear"</span>;</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="dictionary-timinginput-members"><h4><span class="secno">6.5.1 </span>Dictionary <a href="#idl-def-TimingInput" class="idlType"><code>TimingInput</code></a> Members</h4><dl class="dictionary-members"><dt id="widl-TimingInput-startDelay"><code>startDelay</code> of type <span class="idlMemberType"><a>double</a></span>, defaulting to <code>0</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The specified <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start delay</a>.
            </p>
            <p>
              See the description of the <code>startDelay</code> attribute on
              the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingInput-fillMode"><code>fillMode</code> of type <span class="idlMemberType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a></span>, defaulting to <code>"forwards"</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-fill-mode">fill mode</a> as specified by one of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-FillMode"><code>FillMode</code></a>
              enumeration values.
            </p>
            <p class="note">
              Note that in both CSS Animations [<cite><a href="#bib-CSS3-ANIMATIONS" rel="biblioentry" class="bibref">CSS3-ANIMATIONS</a></cite>] and SVG
              [<cite><a href="#bib-SVG112" rel="biblioentry" class="bibref">SVG112</a></cite>] the default fill mode is "none".
              Web Animations differs in this regard since it was determined
              that when generating animations from script, forwards filling is
              the more commonly-desired behavior.
            </p>
            <p class="issue">
              Some feedback suggests the default here should be "both".
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingInput-iterationStart"><code>iterationStart</code> of type <span class="idlMemberType"><a>double</a></span>, defaulting to <code>0.0</code></dt><dd>

            </p>
            <p>
              See the description of the <code>iterationStart</code> attribute
              on the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingInput-iterationCount"><code>iterationCount</code> of type <span class="idlMemberType"><a>unrestricted double</a></span>, defaulting to <code>1.0</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a><a>'s </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-count">iteration count</a> property.
            </p>
            <p>
              See the description of the <code>iterationCount</code> attribute
              on the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface.
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingInput-iterationDuration"><code>iterationDuration</code> of type <span class="idlMemberType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a>DOMString</a>)</span>, defaulting to <code>"auto"</code></dt><dd>

              See the description of the <code>iterationDuration</code>

            </p>
            <p>
              See the description of the <code>playbackRate</code> attribute
              on the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> interface.

              easing effects.

        <div class="section" id="the-fillmode-enumeration">
          <h4><span class="secno">6.5.2 </span>The <code>FillMode</code> enumeration</h4>
          <pre class="idl"><span class="idlEnum" id="idl-def-FillMode">enum <span class="idlEnumName">FillMode</span> {<span class="idlEnumValues"> "<a href="#widl-FillMode-none">none</a>", "<a href="#widl-FillMode-forwards">forwards</a>", "<a href="#widl-FillMode-backwards">backwards</a>", "<a href="#widl-FillMode-both">both</a>" </span>};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="values"><h5><span class="secno">6.5.2.1 </span>Values</h5><dl class="values"><dt id="widl-FillMode-none"><code>none</code></dt><dd>
              No fill.
            </dd><dt id="widl-FillMode-forwards"><code>forwards</code></dt><dd>
              Fill forwards.
            </dd><dt id="widl-FillMode-backwards"><code>backwards</code></dt><dd>
              Fill backwards.
            </dd><dt id="widl-FillMode-both"><code>both</code></dt><dd>
              Fill backwards and forwards.
            </dd></dl></div>
        </div>
        <div class="section" id="the-playbackdirection-enumeration">
          <h4><span class="secno">6.5.3 </span>The <code>PlaybackDirection</code> enumeration</h4>
          <pre class="idl"><span class="idlEnum" id="idl-def-PlaybackDirection">enum <span class="idlEnumName">PlaybackDirection</span> {<span class="idlEnumValues"> "<a href="#widl-PlaybackDirection-normal">normal</a>", "<a href="#widl-PlaybackDirection-reverse">reverse</a>", "<a href="#widl-PlaybackDirection-alternate">alternate</a>", "<a href="#widl-PlaybackDirection-alternate-reverse">alternate-reverse</a>" </span>};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="values-1"><h5><span class="secno">6.5.3.1 </span>Values</h5><dl class="values"><dt id="widl-PlaybackDirection-normal"><code>normal</code></dt><dd>
              All iterations are played as specified.
            </dd><dt id="widl-PlaybackDirection-reverse"><code>reverse</code></dt><dd>
              All iterations are played in the reverse direction from the way
              they are specified.
            </dd><dt id="widl-PlaybackDirection-alternate"><code>alternate</code></dt><dd>
              Even iterations are played as specified, odd iterations are played
              in the reverse direction from the way they are specified.
            </dd><dt id="widl-PlaybackDirection-alternate-reverse"><code>alternate-reverse</code></dt><dd>
              Even iterations are played in the reverse direction from the way
              they are specified, odd iterations are played as specified.
            </dd></dl></div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timinggroup-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.6 </span>The <code>TimingGroup</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          The different types of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing groups</a>
          defined by Web Animations share a common <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a>
          interface as defined below.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-TimingGroup">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">TimingGroup</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItemList"><code>TimedItemList</code></a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimingGroup-children">children</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span>    <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimingGroup-firstChild">firstChild</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span>    <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimingGroup-lastChild">lastChild</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimingGroup-prepend-void-TimedItem...-items">prepend</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>TimedItem...</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">items</span></span>);</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimingGroup-append-void-TimedItem...-items">append</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>TimedItem...</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">items</span></span>);</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-4"><h4><span class="secno">6.6.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-TimingGroup-children"><code>children</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItemList"><code>TimedItemList</code></a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            The list of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed items</a> in the group.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingGroup-firstChild"><code>firstChild</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-first-child">first child</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing group</a>.
          </dd><dt id="widl-TimingGroup-lastChild"><code>lastChild</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-last-child">last child</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-group">timing group</a>.
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-2"><h4><span class="secno">6.6.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-TimingGroup-prepend-void-TimedItem...-items"><code>prepend</code></dt><dd>
            <ol>
              <li>If any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in <var>items</var> is an
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                  throw a <code>HierarchyRequestError</code> exception and
                  terminate these steps. 
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">Insert</a> <var>items</var> before
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-first-child">first child</a>.
            </li></ol>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">items</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>TimedItem...</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd><dt id="widl-TimingGroup-append-void-TimedItem...-items"><code>append</code></dt><dd>
            <ol>
              <li>If any of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in <var>items</var> is an
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-inclusive-ancestor">inclusive ancestor</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                  throw a <code>HierarchyRequestError</code> exception and
                  terminate these steps. 
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">Insert</a> <var>items</var> before
                  <code>null</code>.
            </li></ol>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">items</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>TimedItem...</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a>void</a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
        <div class="section" id="common-definitions-for-manipulating-hierarchies">
          <h4><span class="secno">6.6.3 </span>Common definitions for manipulating hierarchies</h4>
          <p>The <dfn id="dfn-next-sibling-not-included" title="next sibling not included">next sibling of
             <var>item</var> not included</dfn> in a set of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
             items</a>, <var>items</var> is determined using the following
             steps:</p>
          <ol>
            <li>Let <var>context item</var> be <var>item</var>.
            </li><li>While the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-next-sibling">next sibling</a> of <var>context item</var> is not
                <code>null</code> perform the following steps:
              <ol>
                <li>Let <var>context item</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-next-sibling">next sibling</a> of
                    <var>context item</var>.
                </li><li>If <var>context item</var> is not in <var>items</var> return
                    <var>context item</var> and terminate these steps.
              </li></ol>
            </li><li>Return <code>null</code>.
          </li></ol>
          <p>To <dfn id="dfn-remove-a-timed-item" title="remove a timed item">remove</dfn> an <var>item</var>
             its parent or player, perform the steps corresponding to the first
             matching condition from below, if any:
          </p><dl class="switch">
            <dt>If <var>item</var> has a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>,</dt>
            <dd>
              Remove <var>item</var> from the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parent-timing-group">parent timing group</a>'s list
              of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed items</a>.
            </dd>
            <dt>If <var>item</var> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-directly-associated-with-a-player">directly associated with
                a player</a>,</dt>
            <dd>
              Disassociate <var>item</var> from the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>.
            </dd>
          </dl>
          <p>To <dfn id="dfn-insert-children" title="insert children">insert</dfn> a series of zero or
             more <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a>, <var>items</var>, to <var>parent</var>'s
             list of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed items</a> before <var>reference child</var>
             perform the following steps for each <var>item</var> in
             <var>items</var>:</p>
          <ol>
            <li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-remove-a-timed-item" title="remove a timed item">Remove</a> <var>item</var>
                from its parent.
            </li><li>Insert <var>item</var> to <var>parent</var>'s list of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child
                timed items</a> before <var>reference child</var>.
          </li></ol>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-timeditemlist-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.7 </span>The <code>TimedItemList</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          A list of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> may be represented by
          a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItemList"><code>TimedItemList</code></a>.
        </p>
        <p>
          The <code>TimedItemList</code> interface supports indexed
          properties with indices in the range 0 &#x2264; <var>index</var> &lt;
          <code>length</code>. 
        </p>
        <p class="annotation">
          The only reason this interface exists is to provide a familiar
          experience for authors familiar with DOM interfaces where child nodes
          are accessed via a <code>children</code> member.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-TimedItemList">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">TimedItemList</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unsigned long</a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-TimedItemList-length">length</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    getter <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>?</span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-TimedItemList-item-TimedItem-unsigned-long-index">item</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>unsigned long</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">index</span></span>);</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-5"><h4><span class="secno">6.7.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-TimedItemList-length"><code>length</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>unsigned long</a></span>, readonly</dt><dd>
            The number of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed items</a> in the list.
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-3"><h4><span class="secno">6.7.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-TimedItemList-item-TimedItem-unsigned-long-index"><code>item</code> [<em>index</em>]</dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> at <code>index</code>.
              If <code>index</code> is greater than or equal to
              <code>length</code> returns <code>null</code>.
            </p>
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">index</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>unsigned long</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></code>, nullable</div></dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-pargroup-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.8 </span>The <code>ParGroup</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-parallel-timing-group">Parallel timing groups</a> are
          represented by the <code>ParGroup</code> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-ParGroup">[<span class="idlCtor"><span class="idlCtorName"><a href="#widl-ctor-ParGroup--sequence-TimedItem--children--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing">Constructor</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType">sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>&gt;?</span> <span class="idlParamName">children</span></span>, 
              <span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)?</span> <span class="idlParamName">timing</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">null</span></span>)</span>]
interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">ParGroup</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a></span> {
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-ParGroup-clone-ParGroup">clone</a></span> ();</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="constructors"><h4><span class="secno">6.8.1 </span>Constructors</h4><dl class="constructors"><dt id="widl-ctor-ParGroup--sequence-TimedItem--children--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing"><code>ParGroup</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> object using the following
              procedure:
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>Create a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> object, <var>group</var>.</li>
              <li>Set <var>timing input</var> as follows,
                <dl class="switch">
                  <dt>If <var>timing</var> is a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> object,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> refer to <var>timing</var>.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>If <var>timing</var> is a <code>double</code>,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> be a new
                    <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> object with all members set to their
                    default values and <code>iterationDuration</code> set to
                    <var>timing</var>.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>Otherwise (<var>timing</var> is <code>null</code> or
                      undefined),</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> be a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>
                    object with all members set to their default values.
                  </dd>
                </dl>
              </li>
              <li>
                Set <code><var>animation</var>.specified</code> to a new
                <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> object whose attributes are assigned the
                value of the member of the same name on <var>timing input</var>.
                <p class="todo">
                  The above two steps are identical with the constructor for <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> and should be
                  factored out somewhere.
                </p>
              </li>
              <li>
                Add <var>children</var> to the group by calling
                <code><var>group</var>.splice(0, 0,
                <var>children</var>)</code>.
              </li>
            </ol>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that since <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> objects have the same member
                names as <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> dictionaries, it is also possible to
                pass the <code>specified</code> member of another
                <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> as the <var>timing</var> parameter.
              </p>
              <p>
                Doing so will cause the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> object to be treated as
                a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> dictionary and thus it will effectively be
                cloned, not shared.
              </p>
            </div>
            
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">children</td><td class="prmType"><code>sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>&gt;</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc">
                <p>
                  A sequence of timed items to add as children of this group.
                </p>
                <p>
                  These children are appended in sequence using the same
                  semantics as the <code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a>.add</code> method.
                </p>
              </td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">timing</td><td class="prmType"><code>(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>null</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc">
                <p>
                  The timing properties or <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> of the new
                  timing group.
                </p>
              </td></tr></table></dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-4"><h4><span class="secno">6.8.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-ParGroup-clone-ParGroup"><code>clone</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a deep copy of this <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> object using the
              following procedure.
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>Let <var>source</var> be this <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> object, the
                  object to be cloned.</li>
              <li>Let <var>cloned timing</var> be a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>
                  object whose members are assigned the value of the attribute
                  with the same name on
                  <code><var>source</var>.specified</code>.</li>
              <li>Let <var>cloned children</var> be an empty sequence of
                  <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a> objects.</li>
              <li>For each <var>child</var> in
                  <code><var>source</var>.children</code>, append the result
                  of calling <code><var>child</var>.clone()</code>
                  to <var>cloned children</var>.
              </li><li>Return a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> object created by
                  calling the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a> constructor with parameters
                  <code>ParGroup(<var>cloned children</var>,
                  <var>cloned timing</var>)</code>.</li>
            </ol>
          <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-seqgroup-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.9 </span>The <code>SeqGroup</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sequence-timing-group">Sequence timing groups</a> are
          represented by the <code>SeqGroup</code> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-SeqGroup">[<span class="idlCtor"><span class="idlCtorName"><a href="#widl-ctor-SeqGroup--sequence-TimedItem--children--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing">Constructor</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType">sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>&gt;?</span> <span class="idlParamName">children</span></span>, 
              <span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)?</span> <span class="idlParamName">timing</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">null</span></span>)</span>]
interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">SeqGroup</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a></span> {
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-SeqGroup"><code>SeqGroup</code></a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-SeqGroup-clone-SeqGroup">clone</a></span> ();</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="constructors-1"><h4><span class="secno">6.9.1 </span>Constructors</h4><dl class="constructors"><dt id="widl-ctor-SeqGroup--sequence-TimedItem--children--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing"><code>SeqGroup</code></dt><dd>
            The meaning and handling of each of the parameters in this
            constructor is identical to the constructor for
            <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a>.
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">children</td><td class="prmType"><code>sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>&gt;</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">timing</td><td class="prmType"><code>(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>null</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table></dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-5"><h4><span class="secno">6.9.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-SeqGroup-clone-SeqGroup"><code>clone</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a deep copy of this <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-SeqGroup"><code>SeqGroup</code></a> object using the same
              procedure as defined for <a href="#widl-ParGroup-clone-ParGroup">ParGroup.clone</a> except
              that a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-SeqGroup"><code>SeqGroup</code></a> object is created instead of
              a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-ParGroup"><code>ParGroup</code></a>.
            </p>
          <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-SeqGroup"><code>SeqGroup</code></a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-animation-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.10 </span>The <code>Animation</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animations</a> are represented by the
          <code>Animation</code> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-Animation">[<span class="idlCtor"><span class="idlCtorName"><a href="#widl-ctor-Animation--AnimationTarget-element--AnimationEffect-or-CustomEffect-or-OneOrMoreKeyframes--effect--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing">Constructor</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a>?</span> <span class="idlParamName">element</span></span>, 
              <span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType">(<a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a>)?</span> <span class="idlParamName">effect</span></span>, 
              <span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType">(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)?</span> <span class="idlParamName">timing</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">null</span></span>)</span>]
interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">Animation</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a></span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">             attribute <span class="idlAttrType">(<a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a>)?</span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Animation-effect">effect</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    readonly attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a>?</span>                   <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-Animation-target">target</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation"><code>Animation</code></a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-Animation-clone-Animation">clone</a></span> ();</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="constructors-2"><h4><span class="secno">6.10.1 </span>Constructors</h4><dl class="constructors"><dt id="widl-ctor-Animation--AnimationTarget-element--AnimationEffect-or-CustomEffect-or-OneOrMoreKeyframes--effect--unrestricted-double-or-TimingInput--timing"><code>Animation</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> object
              using the following procedure:
            </p>
            <ol>
              <li>Create a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a>
                  object, <var>animation</var>.</li>
              <li>Set the <code>specified</code> member of <var>animation</var>
                  as follows,
                <dl class="switch">
                  <dt>If <var>timing</var> is a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> object,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> refer to <var>timing</var>.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>If <var>timing</var> is a <code>double</code>,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> be a new
                    <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> object with all members set to their
                    default values and <code>iterationDuration</code> set to
                    <var>timing</var>.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>Otherwise (<var>timing</var> is <code>null</code> or
                      undefined),</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Let <var>timing input</var> be a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>
                    object with all members set to their default values.
                  </dd>
                </dl>
              </li>
              <li>
                If <var>timing input</var> is set to a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>
                object,
                set <code><var>animation</var>.specified</code> to a new
                <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> object whose attributes are assigned the
                value of the member of the same name on <var>timing input</var>.
              </li>
              <li>Assign the animation effect based on the type of
                <var>effect</var> as follows,
                <dl class="switch">
                  <dt>If <var>effect</var> is an <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a>
                      object or a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> object,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Assign <code><var>animation</var>.effect</code> to
                    <var>effect</var>.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>If <var>effect</var> is a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a>,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Set <code><var>animation</var>.effect</code> to
                    a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-KeyframeAnimationEffect"><code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code></a> object constructed by
                    passing <var>effect</var> as the <var>frames</var> parameter
                    and with the other parameters set to their default values.
                  </dd>
                  <dt>Otherwise,</dt>
                  <dd>
                    Set <code><var>animation</var>.effect</code> to
                    <code>null</code>.
                  </dd>
                </dl>
              </li>
            </ol>
            <p>
              Examples of the usage of this constructor are given in <a href="#creating-a-new-animation-object" class="sectionRef">section 6.10.4 Creating a new Animation object</a>.
            </p>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that as with <a href="#widl-ctor-TimingEvent--DOMString-type-TimingEventInit-eventInitDict">the
                constructor for </a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingGroup"><code>TimingGroup</code></a>s
                it is possible to pass in a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Timing"><code>Timing</code></a> object here (e.g. the
                <code>specified</code> member of another <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimedItem"><code>TimedItem</code></a>) in
                which case it will be cloned.
              </p>
            </div>
            
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">element</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc">
                The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-target-element">target element</a> or target pseudo-element.
                This may be <code>null</code> for animations that do not target
                a specific element.
              </td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">effect</td><td class="prmType"><code>(<a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a>)</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc">
                The animation effect used to set the <code>effect</code>
                attribute of the newly-created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation
                interface"><code>Animation</code></a> object.
                <p>
                  If this parameter is an <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> object or
                  <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> object, it will shared with any
                  other <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> objects
                  referring to the same <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> or
                  <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> object.
                  It will <em>not</em> be copied.
                </p>
                <p>
                  If this parameter of type <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a>,
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a> of the newly-created
                  <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> will be
                  a newly-created <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-KeyframeAnimationEffect"><code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code></a> object
                  initialized by using this object as the list of
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe">keyframes</a> and with all other parameters set to their
                  default values.
                </p>
                <p>
                  If this parameter is <code>null</code>, the newly-created
                  <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> will also have
                  a <code>null</code> animation effect.
                </p>
              </td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">timing</td><td class="prmType"><code>(<a>unrestricted double</a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>)</code></td><td class="prmNullTrue">&#x2714;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>null</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc">
                <p>
                  The timing properties or <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> of the new
                  animation.
                </p>
              </td></tr></table></dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="attributes-6"><h4><span class="secno">6.10.2 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-Animation-effect"><code>effect</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType">(<a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a>)</span>, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a> or <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-custom-effect">custom effect</a> to apply.
              May be <code>null</code> in which case the animation will produce
              no noticeable effect other than dispatching events (see <a href="#timing-events" class="sectionRef">section 5. Timing events</a>).
            </p>
          </dd><dt id="widl-Animation-target"><code>target</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a></span>, readonly, nullable</dt><dd>
            <p>
              The element or pseudo-element being animated by this object.
              This may be <code>null</code> for animations that do not target
              a specific element such as an animation that produces a sound
              using an audio API.
            </p>
            <p class="note">
              Note that in a future version <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a> may be
              extended to allow targetting, for example, a sequence of elements.
              Therefore, code that is intended to be used with arbitrary
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> objects should test the concrete type of
              <code>target</code> before using it and not assume that it refers
              to an Element.
            </p>
            <p class="issue">
              If SVG is extended to allow multiple targets (using, e.g.,
              <code>select="rect"</code>) then it might be most natural to
              represent that in the API but allowing the <code>target</code> to
              refer to multiple elements.
              It's something that deserves attention for version 1.
            </p>
            </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-6"><h4><span class="secno">6.10.3 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-Animation-clone-Animation"><code>clone</code></dt><dd>
              <p>
                Creates a copy of this <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation
                interface"><code>Animation</code></a> object using the following procedure.
              </p>
              <ol>
                <li>Let <var>source</var> be a the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a> object to
                    clone, that is, this object.</li>
                <li>Let <var>cloned timing</var> be a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a>
                    object whose members are assigned the value of the attribute
                    with the same name on
                    <code><var>source</var>.specified</code>.</li>
                <li>
                  The <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> is cloned depending on the type of
                  <code><var>source</var>.effect</code> as follows,
                  <dl class="switch">
                    <dt>If <code><var>source</var>.effect</code> is an
                        <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> object,</dt>
                    <dd>
                      Let <var>cloned effect</var> be the result of calling
                      <code><var>source</var>.effect.clone()</code>.
                    </dd>
                    <dt>If <code><var>source</var>.effect</code> is a
                        <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CustomEffect"><code>CustomEffect</code></a> object,</dt>
                    <dd>
                      If <code><var>source</var>.effect</code> has a method
                      called <code>clone</code> let <var>cloned effect</var> be
                      the result of calling that method, otherwise let
                      <var>cloned effect</var> be
                      <code><var>source</var>.effect</code>.
                    </dd>
                    <dt>Otherwise,</dt>
                    <dd>
                      Let <var>cloned effect</var> be <code>null</code>.
                    </dd>
                  </dl>
                </li>
                <li>Return a new <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> object created by
                    calling the <a href="#widl-ctor-Animation--AnimationTarget-element-object-effect--double-or-TimingInput--timing">Animation
                    constructor</a> with parameters
                    <code>Animation(<var>source</var>.target, <var>cloned
                    effect</var>, <var>cloned timing</var>)</code>.</li>
              </ol>
            <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation"><code>Animation</code></a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
        <div id="creating-a-new-animation-object" class="informative section">
          <h4><span class="secno">6.10.4 </span>Creating a new <code>Animation</code> object</h4><div class="informative-bg"><p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p>
          <p>
            The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> constructor offers a number of approaches to
            creating a new <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> object.
            At its simplest, an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> object that changes the
            &#x2018;left&#x2019; property of <var>elem</var> to 100 over three
            seconds can be achieved as follows:
          </p>
          <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_keyword">var</span> anim <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> left<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'100px'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span></pre>
          <p>
            The second parameter, representing the animation effect, may specify
            multiple properties, an <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> object, or even
            a callback object.
          </p>
          <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_comment">// Specify multiple properties at once</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> animA <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> left<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'100px'</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> top<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'300px'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Specify multiple frames</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> animA <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_symbol">[</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> left<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'100px'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span> <span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> left<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'300px'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span> <span class="sh_symbol">],</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Share the animation effect of another animation</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> animB <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> animA<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>effect<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Supply a specialized animation effect</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> animC <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">PathAnimationEffect</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span> <span class="sh_symbol">...</span> <span class="sh_symbol">),</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span>

<span class="sh_comment">// Supply a custom script-based animation effect</span>
<span class="sh_keyword">var</span> animC <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span>
  <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> 
    sample<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_keyword">function</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>time<span class="sh_symbol">)</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> 
      <span class="sh_keyword">if</span> <span class="sh_symbol">(</span>time <span class="sh_symbol">!==</span> <span class="sh_keyword">null</span><span class="sh_symbol">)</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span>
        document<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>documentElement<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>currentScale <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_number">1.0</span> <span class="sh_symbol">+</span> time <span class="sh_symbol">*</span> <span class="sh_number">2.0</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>
      <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span> <span class="sh_keyword">else</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span>
        document<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>documentElement<span class="sh_symbol">.</span>currentScale <span class="sh_symbol">=</span> <span class="sh_number">1.0</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span>
      <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span>
    <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span>
    clone<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_keyword">function</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> <span class="sh_keyword">return</span> <span class="sh_keyword">this</span><span class="sh_symbol">;</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span>
  <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span></pre>
          <p class="todo">
            Fill in the parameters for <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PathAnimationEffect"><code>PathAnimationEffect</code></a> above once
            we have decided on them.
          </p>
          <p>
            The third parameter representing the animation's timing, may
            simply be a number representing the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a> as
            above, or, to specify further timing properties such as the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-playback-rate" title="timed item playback rate">playback rate</a>,
            a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-TimingInput"><code>TimingInput</code></a> can be used as follows:
          </p>
          <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_keyword">var</span> anim <span class="sh_symbol">=</span>
  <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> left<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'100px'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> iterationDuration<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_number">3</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> playbackRate<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_number">2</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span></pre>
          <p>
            It is also possible to omit the timing parameter altogether in which
            case default timing values will be used.
            Since the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-intrinsic-iteration-duration">intrinsic iteration duration</a> of an animation is
            zero, and the default <code>fillMode</code> when constructing an
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">Animation</a> is <span class="prop-value">forwards</span>, it is
            possible to create animations that simply set a property without
            any interpolation as follows,
          </p>
          <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> display<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'none'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">);</span></pre>
          <p>
            This is particularly useful in combination with other <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation" title="animation">animations</a> or <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
            items</a>.
            For example, fading an element before switching
            &#x2018;display&#x2019; to &#x2018;none&#x2019; can be achieved as
            follows,
          </p>
          <pre class="example sh_javascript sh_sourceCode"><span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">SeqGroup</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>
  <span class="sh_symbol">[</span>
    <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> opacity<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'0%'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_number">1</span><span class="sh_symbol">),</span>
    <span class="sh_keyword">new</span> <span class="sh_function">Animation</span><span class="sh_symbol">(</span>elem<span class="sh_symbol">,</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">{</span> display<span class="sh_symbol">:</span> <span class="sh_string">'none'</span> <span class="sh_cbracket">}</span><span class="sh_symbol">)</span>
  <span class="sh_symbol">]</span>
<span class="sh_symbol">);</span></pre>
          <p>
            Having created an <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Animation" title="Animation interface"><code>Animation</code></a>, it
            can be played using
            <code>document.timeline.play(<var>anim</var>)</code>.
            For simple effects, the <a href="#extensions-to-the-element-interface"><code>Element.animate</code></a>
            shortcut is more convenient since it performs this last step
            automatically.
          </p>
        </div></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-pseudoelementreference-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.11 </span>The <code>PseudoElementReference</code> interface</h3>
        <p class="issue">
          We should replace this with the <a href="http://dev.w3.org/csswg/cssom/#the-pseudoelement-interface"><code>PseudoElement</code></a>
          from CSSOM unless it gets dropped.
        </p>
        <p>
          Since <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">animations</a> may also target
          pseudo-elements, Web Animations API introduces the
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PseudoElementReference"><code>PseudoElementReference</code></a> interface to represent such targets.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-PseudoElementReference">[<span class="idlCtor"><span class="idlCtorName"><a href="#widl-ctor-PseudoElementReference--Element-element-DOMString-pseudoElement">Constructor</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">element</span></span>, <span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a>DOMString</a></span> <span class="idlParamName">pseudoElement</span></span>)</span>]
interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">PseudoElementReference</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a></span>   <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-PseudoElementReference-element">element</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a>DOMString</a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-PseudoElementReference-pseudoElement">pseudoElement</a></span>;</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="constructors-3"><h4><span class="secno">6.11.1 </span>Constructors</h4><dl class="constructors"><dt id="widl-ctor-PseudoElementReference--Element-element-DOMString-pseudoElement"><code>PseudoElementReference</code></dt><dd>
            Creates a new pseudo-element reference using <var>element</var> as
            the <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-selectors/#subject">subject</a>
            and <var>pseudoElement</var> as the pseudo-element to match (e.g.
            &#x2018;<code>::first-line</code>&#x2019;).
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">element</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">pseudoElement</td><td class="prmType"><code><a>DOMString</a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc"></td></tr></table></dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="attributes-7"><h4><span class="secno">6.11.2 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-PseudoElementReference-element"><code>element</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a></span></dt><dd>
            The element used as the <a href="http://www.w3.org/TR/css3-selectors/#subject">subject</a> for
            matching a pseudo-element.
            <p>Exceptions:</p>
            <dl class="exceptions">
              <dt>DOMException of type
                  <code>NoModificationAllowedError</code></dt>
              <dd>
                Raised on setting if this object is a readonly object.
              </dd>
            </dl>
          </dd><dt id="widl-PseudoElementReference-pseudoElement"><code>pseudoElement</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a>DOMString</a></span></dt><dd>
            The pseudo-element including the initial colon(s). For example,
            &#x2018;<code>::after</code>&#x2019;.
            <p>Exceptions:</p>
            <dl class="exceptions">
              <dt>DOMException of type
                  <code>NoModificationAllowedError</code></dt>
              <dd>
                Raised on setting if this object is a readonly object.
              </dd>
            </dl>
          </dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-animationtarget-typedef">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.12 </span>The <code>AnimationTarget</code> typedef</h3>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlTypedef" id="idl-def-AnimationTarget">typedef <span class="idlTypedefType">(<a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a> or <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PseudoElementReference"><code>PseudoElementReference</code></a>)</span> <span class="idlTypedefID">AnimationTarget</span>;</span>
</pre><div class="idlTypedefDesc">
          For simplicity, throughout this specification <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationTarget"><code>AnimationTarget</code></a>
          is used wherever either an <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Element"><code>Element</code></a> or
          a <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-PseudoElementReference"><code>PseudoElementReference</code></a> can be used.
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-animationeffect-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.13 </span>The <code>AnimationEffect</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">Animation effects</a> are represented by
          the <code>AnimationEffect</code> interface.
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a> is an abstract interface of which several
          concrete subinterfaces are provided.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-AnimationEffect">interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">AnimationEffect</span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-AnimationEffect-accumulate">accumulate</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a></span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-AnimationEffect-clone-AnimationEffect">clone</a></span> ();</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="attributes-8"><h4><span class="secno">6.13.1 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-AnimationEffect-accumulate"><code>accumulate</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-accumulation-operation">accumulation operation</a> property of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation
              effect</a> as specified by one of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a>
              constants.
            </p>
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-7"><h4><span class="secno">6.13.2 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-AnimationEffect-clone-AnimationEffect"><code>clone</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates and returns a new object of the same type as this object's
              most-derived interface such that it will produce the same output
              as this object.
            </p>
            <p class="todo">
              We either need a more rigorous definition here or (probably
              better) a sets of steps on a per-subclass basis.
            </p>
          <div><em>No parameters.</em></div><div><em>Return type: </em><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a></code></div></dd></dl></div>
        <div class="annotation">
          In future, we may expose <code>any sample (double?  timeFraction,
          double currentIteration, AnimationTarget? target, any
          underlyingValue)</code> so that the animation effects can be driven
          apart from the timing model.
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-accumulateoperation-enumeration">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.14 </span>The <code>AccumulateOperation</code> enumeration</h3>
        <p>
          The possible values of an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a>'s
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-accumulation">accumulation</a> behavior are represented by the
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a> enumeration.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlEnum" id="idl-def-AccumulateOperation">enum <span class="idlEnumName">AccumulateOperation</span> {<span class="idlEnumValues"> "<a href="#widl-AccumulateOperation-sum">sum</a>", "<a href="#widl-AccumulateOperation-none">none</a>" </span>};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="values-2"><h4><span class="secno">6.14.1 </span>Values</h4><dl class="values"><dt id="widl-AccumulateOperation-sum"><code>sum</code></dt><dd>
            Corresponds to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-accumulation-operation-sum" title="accumulation operation sum">sum</a>
            accumulation operation value such that
            subsequent iterations of an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation">animation</a> build on the final
            value of the previous iteration.
          </dd><dt id="widl-AccumulateOperation-none"><code>none</code></dt><dd>
            Corresponds to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-accumulation-operation-none" title="accumulation operation none">none</a>
            accumulation operation value such that the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-intermediate-animation-value">intermediate animation
            value</a> produced is independent of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-iteration">current iteration</a>.
          </dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-compositeoperation-enumeration">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.15 </span>The <code>CompositeOperation</code> enumeration</h3>
        <p>
          The possible values of an <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a>'s
          composition behavior are represented by the
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a> enumeration.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlEnum" id="idl-def-CompositeOperation">enum <span class="idlEnumName">CompositeOperation</span> {<span class="idlEnumValues"> "<a href="#widl-CompositeOperation-replace">replace</a>", "<a href="#widl-CompositeOperation-add">add</a>", "<a href="#widl-CompositeOperation-merge">merge</a>" </span>};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="values-3"><h4><span class="secno">6.15.1 </span>Values</h4><dl class="values"><dt id="widl-CompositeOperation-replace"><code>replace</code></dt><dd>
            Corresponds to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation-replace" title="composition operation replace">replace</a>
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a> value such that
            the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a> overrides the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-base-value">base value</a> it is
            combined with.
          </dd><dt id="widl-CompositeOperation-add"><code>add</code></dt><dd>
            Corresponds to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation-add" title="composition operation add">add</a>
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a> value such that
            the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-addition" title="addition">added</a> to
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-base-value">base value</a> it is combined with.
          </dd><dt id="widl-CompositeOperation-merge"><code>merge</code></dt><dd>
            Corresponds to the <a title="composition operation merge">merge</a>
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a> value such that
            the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a> is combined with its <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-base-value">base value</a>
            in a time-dependent fashion.
          </dd></dl></div>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="the-keyframeanimationeffect-interface">
        <h3><span class="secno">6.16 </span>The <code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code> interface</h3>
        <p>
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe-animation-effect">Keyframe animation effects</a> are represented by the
          <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-KeyframeAnimationEffect"><code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code></a> interface.
        </p>
        <pre class="idl"><span class="idlInterface" id="idl-def-KeyframeAnimationEffect">[<span class="idlCtor"><span class="idlCtorName"><a href="#widl-ctor-KeyframeAnimationEffect--OneOrMoreKeyframes-frames-CompositeOperation-composite-AccumulateOperation-accumulate">Constructor</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">frames</span></span>, <span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">composite</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">"replace"</span></span>, 
              <span class="idlParam">optional <span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">accumulate</span> = <span class="idlParamValue">"none"</span></span>)</span>]
interface <span class="idlInterfaceID">KeyframeAnimationEffect</span> : <span class="idlSuperclass"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AnimationEffect"><code>AnimationEffect</code></a></span> {
<span class="idlAttribute">    attribute <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a></span> <span class="idlAttrName"><a href="#widl-KeyframeAnimationEffect-composite">composite</a></span>;</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType">sequence&lt;<a></a><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-Keyframe"><code>Keyframe</code></a>&gt;</span> <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-KeyframeAnimationEffect-getFrames-sequence-Keyframe">getFrames</a></span> ();</span>
<span class="idlMethod">    <span class="idlMethType"><a>void</a></span>               <span class="idlMethName"><a href="#widl-KeyframeAnimationEffect-setFrames-void-OneOrMoreKeyframes-frames">setFrames</a></span> (<span class="idlParam"><span class="idlParamType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a></span> <span class="idlParamName">frames</span></span>);</span>
};</span>
</pre><div class="section" id="constructors-4"><h4><span class="secno">6.16.1 </span>Constructors</h4><dl class="constructors"><dt id="widl-ctor-KeyframeAnimationEffect--OneOrMoreKeyframes-frames-CompositeOperation-composite-AccumulateOperation-accumulate"><code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Creates a new <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-KeyframeAnimationEffect"><code>KeyframeAnimationEffect</code></a> object for the
              given set of keyframes.
            </p>
            <p>
              Before storing, each of the keyframes in <var>frames</var> is
              normalized using the procedure in <a href="#normalizing-a-keyframe-object" class="sectionRef">section 6.17.2 Normalizing a Keyframe object</a>.
            </p>
            
          <table class="parameters"><tr><th>Parameter</th><th>Type</th><th>Nullable</th><th>Optional</th><th>Description</th></tr><tr><td class="prmName">frames</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-OneOrMoreKeyframes"><code>OneOrMoreKeyframes</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt prmOptFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmDesc">
                The set of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe">keyframes</a> used for calculating animation
                values for this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-effect">animation effect</a>.
                The constraints on this parameter and its processing are
                indentical as with <code>setFrames</code>.
              </td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">composite</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>"replace"</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc">
                The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a> used to composite this
                animation with the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-stack">animation stack</a>, as specified by one
                of the <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a> enumeration values.
                This is used for all keyframes that do not specify
                a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a>.
              </td></tr><tr><td class="prmName">accumulate</td><td class="prmType"><code><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-AccumulateOperation"><code>AccumulateOperation</code></a></code></td><td class="prmNullFalse">&#x2718;</td><td class="prmOpt"><span class="prmOptTrue">&#x2714;</span> (<code>"none"</code>)</td><td class="prmDesc">
                The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-accumulation-operation">accumulation operation</a> used to define the way
                animation values build from iteration to iteration.
              </td></tr></table></dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="attributes-9"><h4><span class="secno">6.16.2 </span>Attributes</h4><dl class="attributes"><dt id="widl-KeyframeAnimationEffect-composite"><code>composite</code> of type <span class="idlAttrType"><a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a></span></dt><dd>
            <p>
              The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a> used to composite this animation
              with the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-animation-stack">animation stack</a>, as specified by one of the
              <a class="idlType" href="#idl-def-CompositeOperation"><code>CompositeOperation</code></a> enumeration values.
            </p>
            <p>
              This is used for all keyframes that do not specify
              a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-composition-operation">composition operation</a>.
            </p>
          </dd></dl></div><div class="section" id="methods-8"><h4><span class="secno">6.16.3 </span>Methods</h4><dl class="methods"><dt id="widl-KeyframeAnimationEffect-getFrames-sequence-Keyframe"><code>getFrames</code></dt><dd>
            <p>
              Returns the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe">keyframes</a> that make up this effect as
              a sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe">Keyframe</a> objects.
            </p>
            <p>
              Note that the normalization applied to the <em>list</em> of
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-keyframe">keyframes</a> as defined in <a href="#normalizing-the-list-of-keyframes" class="sectionRef">section 6.16.4 Normalizing the list of keyframes</a> does not affect the value returned by this
              method.
            </p>
