    <div id="algorithms-for-path-animation-effects" class="appendix informative section">
      <!--OddPage--><h2><span class="secno">B. </span>Algorithms for path animation effects</h2><div class="informative-bg"><p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p>
      <p class="todo">Write me</p>
    </div></div>

    <div id="algorithms-for-event-dispatch" class="appendix informative section">
      <!--OddPage--><h2><span class="secno">C. </span>Algorithms for event dispatch</h2><div class="informative-bg"><p><em>This section is non-normative.</em></p>
      <p>
        The following algorithms demonstrate a possible approach to handling
        event queuing that incorporates the various requirements outlined in <a href="#timing-events" class="sectionRef">section 5. Timing events</a>.
      </p>
      <p>
        Some of the features of the following approach are:
      </p>
      <ul>
        <li>Sorts only once per timeline.
        </li><li>Handles cotemporal samples without dispatching duplicate events.
        </li><li>Handles zero-length intervals.
        </li><li>Stores sample state only at the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> level.
            (The <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a> is still per-<a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
            however.)
            This makes it possible for an implementation to optimize
            the case when there are no registered event listeners on part of the
            timing hierarchy.
            In such a case the whole procedure for determining and dispatching
            events can be skipped for that part of the hierarchy.
            Should event listeners be attached at a later point, the
            state stored at the player can be used to ensure the previously
            ignored timed items begin providing events as if they had always had
            event listeners.
      </li></ul>
      <div class="section" id="interval-boundaries-and-time-marks">
        <h3><span class="secno">C.1 </span>Interval boundaries and time marks</h3>
        <p>
          With regards to event dispatch, interval boundary conditions are
          particularly important.
          For example, if we were to conduct a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-sample">sample</a> at time 3s and then
          another sample at 5s, on that second sample we should dispatch all
          events between the two times.
          If a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> were to start at time 5s, then we
          should dispatch the corresponding <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingstart">timingstart</a> event since that
          time has arrived.
          However, since we will have already dispatched all events at time 3s
          during the previous sample, we should <em>not</em> dispatch any events
          coinciding with time 3s.
        </p>
        <p>
          In other situations, however, such as when getting the events
          scheduled by <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed items</a> within a given iteration, we
          should include <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingstart">timingstart</a> events that coincide with the start
          of the iteration but not <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a> events since, under Web
          Animations endpoint-exclusive timing model, those <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a>
          events happened fractionally before the iteration started.
          To accommodate these different endpoint behaviors we introduce the
          concept of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a>.
        </p>
        <p>
          A <dfn id="dfn-time-mark">time mark</dfn> is a triple consisting of:
        </p>
        <ul>
          <li>a <span class="property">time value</span>,
          </li><li>a <span class="property">position</span>: <span class="position">minus</span>, <span class="position">zero</span>,
            or <span class="position">plus</span>, and
          </li><li>a Boolean flag indicating if the mark represents the endpoint of
              an interval or not (regardless of which &#x2018;end&#x2019; of the
              interval the mark represents)
        </li></ul>
        <p>
          We can use subscript notation to indicate these properties.
          For example, <var class="timeMark">t<sub>minus|end</sub></var>.
          If the time mark does not represent an interval endpoint, the
          &#x2018;|end&#x2019; part of the subscript text is dropped, as in
          <var class="timeMark">t<sub>minus</sub></var>.
        </p>
        <p>
          For a given <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>, |<var class="timeMark">t</var>|
          indicates just the <span class="property">time value</span> ignoring
          the other properties, and <var class="timeMark">t<sub>pos</sub></var>
          indicates just the <span class="property">position</span>.
        </p>
        <p>
          The <span class="position">minus</span> position represents a value
          an infinitely small amount less than the <span class="property">time
          value</span> whilst the <span class="position">plus</span> position
          represents a value infinitely small amount greater.
          <span class="position">zero</span> represents the moment at the time
          value.
        </p>
        <p>
          The meaning of these <span class="property">position</span> values is
          not affected by the direction in which playback proceeds.
          We can compare <span class="property">positions</span> and <span class="property">time values</span> as follows:
        </p>
        <p>
          For two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> <var class="timeMark">a</var> and <var class="timeMark">b</var>, <var class="timeMark">a</var> is less than
          <var class="timeMark">b</var> if one of the following conditions is
          true:
        </p>
        <ul>
          <li>|<var class="timeMark">a</var>| &lt;
              |<var class="timeMark">b</var>|, or
          </li><li>|<var class="timeMark">a</var>| =
              |<var class="timeMark">b</var>| and
              <var class="timeMark">a<sub>pos</sub></var> =
              <span class="position">before</span> and
              <var class="timeMark">b<sub>pos</sub></var> &#x2260;
              <span class="position">before</span>, or
          </li><li>|<var class="timeMark">a</var>| =
              |<var class="timeMark">b</var>| and
              <var class="timeMark">a<sub>pos</sub></var>=
              <span class="position">zero</span> and
              <var class="timeMark">b<sub>pos</sub></var>=
              <span class="position">after</span>
        </li></ul>
        <p>
          For two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> <var class="timeMark">a</var> and <var class="timeMark">b</var>, <var class="timeMark">a</var> equals 
          <var class="timeMark">b</var> if
          |<var class="timeMark">a</var>| equals |<var class="timeMark">b</var>|
          and
          <var class="timeMark">a<sub>pos</sub></var> equals
          <var class="timeMark">b<sub>pos</sub></var>.
        </p>
        <p>
          Operations such as greater-than and less-than-or-equal can be
          extrapolated from these definitions.
        </p>
        <p>
          Since these operations only apply to the <span class="property">position</span> and <span class="property">time
          value</span> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>, we define
          the <code><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-first-a-b" title="first(a,b)">first</a>()</code> and
          <code><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-last-a-b" title="last(a,b)">last</a>()</code> operations which are
          for most purposes equivalent to <code>min()</code> and
          <code>max()</code> but in the case where the two arguments are equal,
          it preserves their order.
          Their definitions are as follows.
        </p>
        <ul>
          <li><dfn id="dfn-first-a-b" title="first(a,b)">first</dfn>(<var class="timeMark">a</var>,<var class="timeMark">b</var>) =
              <var class="timeMark">a</var> if <var class="timeMark">a</var>
              &#x2264; <var class="timeMark">b</var> and
              <var class="timeMark">b</var> otherwise.
          </li><li><dfn id="dfn-last-a-b" title="last(a,b)">last</dfn>(<var class="timeMark">a</var>,<var class="timeMark">b</var>) =
              <var class="timeMark">a</var> if <var class="timeMark">a</var>
              &gt; <var class="timeMark">b</var> and
              <var class="timeMark">b</var> otherwise.
        </li></ul>
        <p>
          Given an interval delimited by two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> <var class="timeMark">a</var> and <var class="timeMark">b</var>,
          a time <var>t</var> is <dfn id="dfn-in-the-interval-ab">in the interval <var>ab</var></dfn> if the
          following relationship holds:
          <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-first-a-b" title="first(a,b)">first</a><a>(<var class="timeMark">a</var>,
                                         <var class="timeMark">b</var>)
          &#x2264; <var>t</var>
          &#x2264; </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-last-a-b" title="last(a,b)">last</a><a>(<var class="timeMark">a</var>,
                                            <var class="timeMark">b</var>).
        </a></p><a>
        </a><p><a>
          A </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a> can be added to a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> by simply
          adding the time value components and keeping the <span class="property">position</span> and interval
          endpoint state of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>.
          Addition of two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> is not defined.
        </p>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="events-when-sampling-a-timeline">
        <h3><span class="secno">C.2 </span>Events when sampling a timeline</h3>
        <p>
          For a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a>, <a>sampled</a> such that the current <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time
          value</a> is <var>t</var>, the set of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing events</a> to queue
          can be determined as follows:
        </p>
        <ol>
          <li>Iterate over each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> in the set of players 
            <!-- <a link="associated with a timeline"> -->
            associated<!-- </a> --> with this
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> in the order in which the players were created
            starting from the first created to the last, and for each
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>, perform the steps defined in
            <a href="#event-dispatch-and-unattached-timed-items" class="sectionRef">section 5.7.4 Event dispatch and unattached timed items</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var>events</var> be an empty sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing
              events</a>.
          </li><li>Iterate over each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> in the set of players i
            <!-- <a link="associated with a timeline"> -->
            associated<!-- </a> --> with this
            <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> in the order in which the players were created
            starting from the first created to the last and
            get the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-player-at-timeline-time-t" title="partially ordered set of events for a player at timeline time
            t">partially ordered set of events for the player</a> at
            <var>t</var> and append then to <var>events</var>.
          </li><li>Perform a stable sort on <var>events</var> by <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline
              time</a> such that earlier times sort first.</li>
          <li>Add <var>events</var> to the event queue in their current
              order.</li>
        </ol>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="events-when-sampling-a-player">
        <h3><span class="secno">C.3 </span>Events when sampling a player</h3>
        <p>
          The <dfn id="dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-player-at-timeline-time-t">partially ordered set of events for a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> at
          timeline time <var>t</var></dfn>, can be determined as follows:
        </p>
        <ol>
          <li>Let <var>previous sample mark</var> be a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>
              associated with the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> that is initialized to <span class="timeMark">0<sub>zero|end</sub></span> when the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> is first created.
          </li><li>Let <var>sample time</var> be the result of calculating the
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a>&#x2019;s <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-time">current time</a> at timeline time <var>t</var>.
          </li><li>Let <var>sample mark</var> be <var class="timeMark">sample
              time<sub>plus</sub></var>.
          </li><li>Let <var>events</var> be an empty sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing
              events</a>.
          </li><li>
            The events queued depends on whether or not the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted
            flag</a> is set as follows,
            <dl class="switch">
              <dt>If the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a> of the
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> is set,</dt>
              <dd>
                <ol>
                  <li>If this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> has associated <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source
                      content</a>, then get the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-seeked-to-time-t" title="partially ordered set of events for a timed item seeked to time t">partially
                      ordered set of events scheduled for seek time <var>sample
                      time</var></a> and append them to <var>events</var>.
                  </li><li>Clear the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-adjusted-flag">time adjusted flag</a>.
                </li></ol>
              </dd>
              <dt>Otherwise,</dt>
              <dd>
                <ol>
                  <li>If this <a>player has associated </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-source-content">source content</a>,
                    then get the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-scheduled-between-time-marks-a-and-b" title="partially ordered set of events for a timed item scheduled between time marks a and b">partially
                    ordered set of events scheduled between <var>previous sample
                    mark</var> and <var>sample mark</var></a> and append them to
                    <var>events</var>.
                </li></ol>
              </dd>
            </dl>
            <div class="note">
              <p>
                Note that this approach should correctly handle consecutive
                samples with the same time value.
              </p>
              <p>
                In such a case, both <var>previous sample mark</var> and
                <var>sample mark</var> will have a <span class="property">position</span> of <span class="position">plus</span>.
                Since no <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing events</a> are scheduled to be
                dispatched at the <span class="position">plus</span> position
                there should be no duplicate events.
              </p>
            </div>
          </li><li>Set <var>previous sample mark</var> to <var>sample mark</var>.
          </li><li>Return <var>events</var>.
        </li></ol>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="events-for-a-timed-item-during-regular-sampling">
        <h3><span class="secno">C.4 </span>Events for a timed item during regular sampling</h3>
        <p>
          The <dfn id="dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-scheduled-between-time-marks-a-and-b">partially ordered set of events for a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
          scheduled between time marks <var>a</var> and <var>b</var></dfn>,
          expressed in <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-timing" title="uneased timing">uneased inherited time</a>, can
          be determined as follows:
        </p>
        <ol>
          <li>Let <var>events</var> be an empty sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing
              events</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">range a</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>
              resulting from calculating <var class="timeMark">a</var> + <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-start-time" title="timed item start time">start time</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">range b</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>
              resulting from calculating <var class="timeMark">b</var> + <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item-start-time" title="timed item start time">start time</a>.
          </li><li>Define a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a> <var class="timeMark">t</var> as being
              <dfn id="dfn-in-range">in range</dfn> if it is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-the-interval-ab" title="in the interval ab">in the
              interval</a> (<var class="timeMark">range a</var>,
              <var class="timeMark">range b</var>).
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">range lhs</var> be <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-first-a-b" title="first(a,b)">first</a>(<var class="timeMark">range a</var>,
              <var class="timeMark">range b</var>).
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">range rhs</var> be <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-last-a-b" title="last(a,b)">last</a>(<var class="timeMark">range a</var>,
              <var class="timeMark">range b</var>).
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">active start</var> be <var class="timeMark">start delay<sub>zero|end</sub></var>.
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">active end</var> be <span class="timeMark">(<a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-start-delay">start delay</a> + <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active-duration">active
              duration</a>)<sub>minus|end</sub></span>.
          </li><li>If |<var class="timeMark">active start</var>| = |<var class="timeMark">active end</var>| then set the <span class="property">position</span> of <var class="timeMark">active end</var> to <span class="position">zero</span>.
          </li><li>If either of the following conditions is true:
            <ul><li><var class="timeMark">active end</var> &lt;
                <var class="timeMark">range lhs</var>; or
                </li><li><var class="timeMark">active start</var> &gt;
                <var class="timeMark">range rhs</var>
            </li></ul>
            return <var>events</var>.
          </li><li>If |<var class="timeMark">active start</var>| =
              |<var class="timeMark">active end</var>| and the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed
              item</a>&#x2019;s <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-count">iteration count</a> is infinity, let
              <var>effective iteration count</var> be 1, otherwise let it be
              the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>&#x2019;s <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-count">iteration count</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var>iteration times</var> be a sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time
              values</a> populated with the results of calculating |<var class="timeMark">active start</var>| + <var>i</var> * <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration
              duration</a> for each integer <var>i</var> in the range 0 &lt;
              <var>i</var> &lt; <var>effective iteration count</var>.
          </li><li>Remove all <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time values</a> from <var>iteration times</var>
              where <var class="timeMark">time value<sub>zero</sub></var> is not
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-range">in range</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var>subintervals</var> be an empty sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time
              marks</a>.
          </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">active start</var> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-range">in range</a>,
              append it to <var>subintervals</var>, otherwise append <var class="timeMark">range lhs</var>.
          </li><li>For each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> <var>t</var> in <var>iteration
              times</var>, add the following two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> to
              <var>subintervals</var>, in order,
              <var class="timeMark">t<sub>minus|end</sub></var>,
              <var class="timeMark">t<sub>zero|end</sub></var>
              unless the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration duration</a>
              is zero, in which case add
              <var class="timeMark">t<sub>zero|end</sub></var>,
              <var class="timeMark">t<sub>zero|end</sub></var> instead.
          </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">active end</var> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-range">in range</a>,
              append it to <var>subintervals</var>, otherwise append <var class="timeMark">range rhs</var>.
          </li><li>If the first pair of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> in <var>subintervals</var>
              are not in order, that is, if <var class="timeMark">subintervals[0]</var> &gt; <var class="timeMark">subintervals[1]</var>, remove those two <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time
              marks</a> from <var>subintervals</var>.
              <p class="note">
                This will happen if a non-zero-duration iteration ends at |<var class="timeMark">range lhs</var>| and the <span class="property">position</span> of <var class="timeMark">range
                lhs</var> is not <span class="position">minus</span>.
              </p>
          </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">range a</var> &lt; <var class="timeMark">range b</var>, let <var>direction</var> be
              <span class="prop-value">forwards</span>, otherwise let
              <var>direction</var> be <span class="prop-value">backwards</span>.
          </li><li>If <var>direction</var> is <span class="prop-value">backwards</span>, reverse the elements of
              <var>subintervals</var>.
          </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">directed active start</var> be <var class="timeMark">active start</var> if <var>direction</var> is
              <span class="prop-value">forwards</span> and <var class="timeMark">active end</var> otherwise.
          </li><li>Likewise, let <var class="timeMark">directed active end</var> be
              <var class="timeMark">active end</var> if <var>direction</var> is
              <span class="prop-value">forwards</span> and <var class="timeMark">active start</var> otherwise.
          </li><li>Define the <dfn id="dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t">iteration index at local <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>
              <var class="timeMark">t</var></dfn> as follows:
            <ol>
              <li>Let <var>iteration index</var> be the result of calculating
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-iteration">current iteration</a> at |<var class="timeMark">t</var>|.
              </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">t<sub>pos</sub></var> is <span class="position">minus</span> and (<var>iteration index</var>
                  &#x2001;E<var class="timeMark">active start</var>) % <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-duration">iteration
                  duration</a> = 0,
                  let <var>iteration index</var> be max(0, <var>iteration
                  index</var> - 1).
              </li><li>The result is <var>iteration index</var>.
            </li></ol>
          </li><li>Define the <dfn id="dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t">timeline time at local time <var>t</var></dfn> as
              follows:
            <ol>
              <li>Let the <var>uneased local root time</var> be the result of
                  repeatedly applying the procedures for calculating the
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-inherited-time-from-uneased-local-time">uneased inherited time from uneased local time</a> and
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-local-time-from-uneased-child-time">uneased local time from uneased child time</a>
                  defined in
                  <a href="#inverse-timing-calculations" class="sectionRef">section 5.3 Inverse timing calculations</a>
                  for each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-ancestor">ancestor</a> of this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> in turn up
                  to the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-root">root</a> <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> using <var>t</var> as the
                  initial <var>uneased local time</var>.
              </li><li>Let the <var>uneased local player time</var> be the result of
                  calculating the
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-inherited-time-from-uneased-local-time">uneased inherited time from uneased local time</a> for
                  the <var>uneased local root time</var> using the <var>uneased
                  local root time as the <var>uneased local time</var>.
              </var></li><li>Let the <var>timeline time</var> be the result of calculating
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-from-the-current-time-of-a-player">timeline time from the current time of a player</a> for
                  the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-player">player</a> with which this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> is <a title="associated with a player">associated</a> using the
                  <var>uneased local player time</var> as the <var>current
                  time</var>.
              </li><li>If the <var>timeline time</var> is undefined, let
                  <var>timeline time</var> use the current
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-value">time value</a> of the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline">timeline</a> with which this
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-associated-with-a-timeline" title="associated with
                  a timeline">associated</a>.
              </li><li>The result is <var>timeline time</var>.
            </li></ol>
          </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">directed active start</var> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-range">in
              range</a>, append to <var>events</var> a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a>
              with the following parameters:
            <ul>
              <li>type: <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingstart">timingstart</a>
              </li><li>event target: this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-local-time">event local time</a>:
                  |<var class="timeMark">directed active start</var>|
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline time</a>:
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t" title="timeline time at local time t">timeline
                  time for |<var class="timeMark">directed active
                  start</var>|</a>.
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-iteration-index">event iteration index</a>:
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t" title="iteration index at local time mark t">iteration
                  index at <var class="timeMark">directed active
                  start</var></a>
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-dispatch-flag">seeked dispatch flag</a>: false
            </li></ul>
            Alternatively, if <var class="timeMark">range a</var> is an
            interval endpoint, append a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a> to
            <var>events</var> as above but substituting <var class="timeMark">range a</var> in place of <var class="timeMark">directed active start</var>.
          </li><li>Let <var>subinterval iteration index</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t" title="iteration index at local time mark t">iteration index
            at the first </a><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a> in <var>subintervals</var>.
          </li><li>Let <var>first iteration</var> be <code>true</code>
          </li><li>Iterate over each pair of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a> in
              <var>subintervals</var> in order such that each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time mark</a>
              is used only once.
              For each pair of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time marks</a>,
              (<var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var>,
              <var class="timeMark">subinterval end</var>)
              perform the following steps:
            <ol>
              <li>Let <var>subinterval iteration index</var> be the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t" title="iteration index at local time mark t">iteration index
                at <var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var></a>.
              </li><li>If <em>either</em> of the following conditions is true,
                <ul>
                  <li><var>first iteration</var> is <code>false</code>, or
                  </li><li><var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var> =
                      <var class="timeMark">range a</var> &#x2260;
                      <var class="timeMark">subinterval end</var>
                </li></ul>
                append a new <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a> to <var>events</var> with the
                following paramters:
                <ul>
                  <li>type: <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingiteration">timingiteration</a>
                  </li><li>event target: this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                  </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-local-time">event local time</a>:
                      |<var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var>|
                  </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline time</a>:
                      <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t" title="timeline time at local time t">timeline
                      time for |<var class="timeMark">subinterval
                      start</var>|</a>.
                  </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-iteration-index">event iteration index</a>:
                      <var>subinterval iteration index</var>
                  </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-dispatch-flag">seeked dispatch flag</a>: false
                </li></ul>
              </li><li>Let <var class="timeMark">child start</var> be a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-time-mark">time
                mark</a> whose <span class="property">time value</span> is the
                result of calculating the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-directed-time">directed time</a> corresponding
                to |<var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var>| but using
                <var>subinterval iteration index</var> as the <var>current
                iteration value</var> and assuming a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-fill-mode">fill mode</a> of
                <span class="prop-value">none</span> and whose <span class="property">position</span> is the same as that of <var class="timeMark">subinterval start</var>.
              </li><li>Likewise, let <var class="timeMark">child end</var> be the
                result of performing the same operation but for <var class="timeMark">subinterval end</var>.
              </li><li>Let <var>child direction</var> be
                <span class="prop-value">forwards</span> if
                |<var class="timeMark">child start</var>| &lt;
                |<var class="timeMark">child end</var>|,
                <span class="prop-value">backwards</span> if
                |<var class="timeMark">child start</var>| &gt;
                |<var class="timeMark">child end</var>|,
                and <code>null</code> if
                |<var class="timeMark">child start</var>| =
                |<var class="timeMark">child end</var>|.
              </li><li>If <var>child direction</var> is not <code>null</code> and is
                not equal to <var>direction</var>, invert the <span class="property">position</span> of <var class="timeMark">child start</var> and <var class="timeMark">child end</var> each such that <span class="position">plus</span> becomes <span class="position">minus</span>, and vice versa, and <span class="position">zero</span> remains
                unchanged.
              </li><li>Let <var>child events</var> be an empty sequence of
                <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing events</a>.
              </li><li>Iterate over each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed item</a> in order and for
                each child get the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-scheduled-between-time-marks-a-and-b" title="partially ordered set of events for a timed item scheduled between time marks a and b">partially
                ordered set of events scheduled between <var class="timeMark">child start</var> and <var class="timeMark">child end</var></a> and append to <var>child
                events</var>.
              </li><li>Append <var>child events</var> to <var>events</var>.
              </li><li>If <var>direction</var> is <span class="prop-value">forwards</span>, increment
                  <var>subinterval iteration index</var>, otherwise decrement
                  it.
                  <p class="note">
                    This manual handling of the <var>subinterval iteration
                      index</var> (as opposed to simply recalculating the
                    <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t" title="iteration index at local time mark t">iteration
                    index for each <var>subinterval start</var></a> is
                    necessary for handling zero-length intervals.
                  </p>
              </li><li>Let <var>first iteration</var> be <code>false</code>.
            </li></ol>
          </li><li>If <var class="timeMark">directed active end</var> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-in-range">in
              range</a>, append to <var>events</var> a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a>
              with the following parameters:
            <ul>
              <li>type: <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a>
              </li><li>event target: this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-local-time">event local time</a>:
                  |<var class="timeMark">directed active end</var>|
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline time</a>:
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t" title="timeline time at local time t">timeline
                  time for |<var class="timeMark">directed active
                  end</var>|</a>.
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-iteration-index">event iteration index</a>:
                  <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-iteration-index-at-local-time-mark-t" title="iteration index at local time mark t">iteration
                  index at <var class="timeMark">directed active
                  end</var></a>
              </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-dispatch-flag">seeked dispatch flag</a>: false
            </li></ul>
            Alternatively, if <var class="timeMark">range b</var> is an
            interval endpoint, append a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a> to
            <var>events</var> as above but substituting <var class="timeMark">range b</var> in place of <var class="timeMark">directed active end</var>.
          </li><li>Return <var>events</var>.
        </li></ol>
      </div>
      <div class="section" id="events-for-a-timed-item-during-seeked-event-dispatch">
        <h3><span class="secno">C.5 </span>Events for a timed item during seeked event dispatch</h3>
        <p>
          The <dfn id="dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-seeked-to-time-t">partially ordered set of events for a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
          seeked to time <var>t</var></dfn>, expressed in <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-uneased-timing" title="uneased timing">uneased inherited time</a>,
          can be determined as follows:
        </p>
        <ol>
          <li>Let <var>events</var> be an empty sequence of <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing
              events</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var>local t</var> be <var>t</var> + <a>start time</a>.
          </li><li>Let <var>child time</var> be a <var>time value</var> that is the
              result of calculating the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-directed-time">directed time</a> corresponding to
              <var>local t</var> assuming a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-fill-mode">fill mode</a> of <span class="prop-value">none</span>.
          </li><li>Iterate over each <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-child-timed-item">child timed item</a> in order and for each
              child get the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-partially-ordered-set-of-events-for-a-timed-item-seeked-to-time-t" title="partially ordered set of events for a timed item seeked to time t">partially
              ordered set of events for seek time <var>child time</var></a>
              and append to <var>events</var>.
          </li><li>Let <var>current active state</var> be the result of evaluating if
              this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> is <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-active">active</a> at time <var>local
              t</var>.
          </li><li>If this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> has a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a> of
              <em>inactive</em>, and a <var>current active state</var> of
              <em>active</em>, add to the beginning of <var>events</var> a new
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a> with the following parameters:
              <ul>
                <li>type: <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingstart">timingstart</a>
                </li><li>event target: this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-local-time">event local time</a>: <var>local t</var>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline time</a>:
                    <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t" title="timeline time at local time t">timeline
                    time for <var>local t</var></a>.
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-iteration-index">event iteration index</a>:
                    the result of calculating the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-iteration">current iteration</a> at 
                    at <var>local t</var>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-dispatch-flag">seeked dispatch flag</a>: true
              </li></ul>
          </li><li>If this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a> has a <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-previous-active-state">previous active state</a>
              of <em>active</em>, and a <var>current active state</var> of
              <em>inactive</em>, append to the end of <var>events</var> a new
              <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timing-event">timing event</a> with the following parameters:
              <ul>
                <li>type: <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timingend">timingend</a>
                </li><li>event target: this <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timed-item">timed item</a>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-local-time">event local time</a>: <var>local t</var>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-timeline-time">event timeline time</a>:
                    <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-timeline-time-at-local-time-t" title="timeline time at local time t">timeline
                    time for <var>local t</var></a>.
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-event-iteration-index">event iteration index</a>:
                    the result of calculating the <a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-current-iteration">current iteration</a> at 
                    at <var>local t</var>
                </li><li><a class="internalDFN" href="#dfn-seeked-dispatch-flag">seeked dispatch flag</a>: true
              </li></ul>
          </li><li>Return <var>events</var>.
        </li></ol>
      </div>
    </div></div>
